--- Commit Message ---
LU-15722 osd-ldiskfs: fix write stuck for 64K PAGE_SIZE

This reverts a previous commit for large PAGE_SIZE to fix a stuck IO
issue in another way.

One more ldiskfs_map_blocks() can't fix the write stuck for PAGE_SIZE
> BLOCK_SIZE. It still gets stuck in some tests like sanity-dom fsx.
Because each time ldiskfs_map_blocks() lookup it only return a
continuous range physical blocks. If a page has multiple continuous
range blocks, then it needs multiple ldiskfs_map_blocks() lookups to
find out all the already mapped blocks.

The fixed idea here is to record the already written blocks of the
start page and skip them at the next write retry.

This also fix and cleanup osd_mark_page_io_done() when start_blocks
is non-zero.

Fixes: 176ea3a4599e ("LU-15722 osd-ldiskfs: fix IO write gets stuck for	64K PAGE_SIZE")

Ping.
Note that this patch should not affect 4K page size. because dr_start_pg_wblks always is 0 if 4K page size.
iobuf->dr_start_pg_wblks = (start_blocks + count) % blocks_per_page;

--- Message (Andreas Dilger, 2022-08-26 05:28:58.000000000) ---
Patch Set 15:

> Found very hard to get a Maloo +1. retry again and again with BUILD
 > or rebase?

It is possible to retrigger failed test sessions for known intermittent failures, but this must be done within 7 days of the original patch submission, otherwise the builds are deleted.  We require a patch to pass all tests before it is landed, to avoid regressions.

Since this patch was built and tested on 08-10, the failed sessions can no longer be retested and must be rebuilt and run through all of the tests again.  That should be avoided as much as possible, since it is wasteful of testing resources.
